<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://github.com/AryanVBW/RDPtown/releases/download/l1/rdp2-removebg-preview.png"><img src="https://github.com/AryanVBW/RDPtown/releases/download/l1/rdp2-removebg-preview.png" height="" style="max-width: 100%;"></a><br>
🌟 Free Cloud Linxie RDP🚀
</p>
<p dir="auto">Welcome to the magical world of Linxie – your free Linux Remote Desktop (RDP) and virtual computer ! 🎉
These cloud computers are fully managed by Google, so you can be sure they are reliable and secure. You can use them for anything you want.</p>
<h2 tabindex="-1" id="user-content-features-" dir="auto"><a class="heading-link" href="#features-">Features ✨<svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Virtual Computer: ⚡️ 400MB/ps internet speed</li>
<li>Trustworthy: 🛡️ Hosted and maintained by the  Google</li>
<li>Usage: 👨‍💻 Linux tools, apchee/ngnix, ethical security testing, gaming, and more!</li>
<li>Free forever</li>
<li>Fully managed by Google</li>
<li>Reliable and secure</li>
<li>🖥️ 4GB RAM (Old Gmail accounts get a whooping 16GB RAM!)</li>
<li>Access from any device with an RDP client</li>
</ul>
<h2 tabindex="-1" id="user-content-benefits" dir="auto"><a class="heading-link" href="#benefits">Benefits:<svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Use Linux tools and apps on any device</li>
<li>Develop and test software in a cloud environment</li>
<li>Run hacking exploits safely and securely</li>
<li>Play Linux games without having to install anything</li>
<li>Have your own personal cloud lab</li>
</ul>
<h2 tabindex="-1" id="user-content-how-to-get-free-rdp" dir="auto"><a class="heading-link" href="#how-to-get-free-rdp">How to Get FREE RDP🚀<svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></h2>
<p dir="auto">To use Gmail Cloud Computer, you need to follow these steps:</p>
<h1 tabindex="-1" id="user-content-step-one" dir="auto"><a class="heading-link" href="#step-one">Step ONE<svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></h1>
 - Download Google Cloud app or Go to <a href="https://shell.cloud.google.com" rel="nofollow">shell.cloud.google.com</a> and sign in with your Google account.
<p align="center" dir="auto">
   <a href="https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.google.android.apps.cloudconsole" rel="nofollow">
      <img src="https://github.com/AryanVBW/RDPtown/releases/download/l1/playstore.png" height="60" alt="Darkside" style="max-width: 100%;">
   </a>
</p>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
   <a href="https://apps.apple.com/us/app/google-cloud/id1005120814" rel="nofollow">
      <img src="https://github.com/AryanVBW/RDPtown/releases/download/l1/appstore.png" height="90" alt="Darkside" style="max-width: 100%;">
   </a>
</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Choose a Gmail account that you want to use as your cloud computer. You can use any Gmail account, but older accounts have more RAM and storage space.</li>
</ul>
<h1 tabindex="-1" id="user-content-step-two" dir="auto"><a class="heading-link" href="#step-two">Step TWO<svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></h1>
<h4 tabindex="-1" id="user-content-open-gogogle-cloud-app-on-your-iphone-or-android" dir="auto"><a class="heading-link" href="#open-gogogle-cloud-app-on-your-iphone-or-android">Open gogogle cloud app on your iphone or Android<svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></h4><h4 tabindex="-1" id="user-content-----------click-the-terminalshell-iconwait-for-a-few-minutes-while-the-google-cloud-sets-up-your-cloud-computer-you-will-see-a-terminal-window-when-it-is-ready" dir="auto"><a class="heading-link" href="#----------click-the-terminalshell-iconwait-for-a-few-minutes-while-the-google-cloud-sets-up-your-cloud-computer-you-will-see-a-terminal-window-when-it-is-ready">

<ul dir="auto">
<li>Wait for a few minutes while the Google Cloud sets up your cloud computer. You will see a terminal window when it is ready.</li>
</ul>
<svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></h4><h1 tabindex="-1" id="user-content-step-three" dir="auto"><a class="heading-link" href="#step-three">Step THREE<svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></h1>
 <h4 tabindex="-1" id="user-content-copy-paste-the-following-cammand-one-by-one" dir="auto"><a class="heading-link" href="#copy-paste-the-following-cammand-one-by-one">Copy paste the following cammand one by one<svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></h4>
1.paste this after complet this paste second 
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=" sudo apt update -y &amp;&amp; sudo apt upgrade -y
 sudo apt install wget -y"><pre> sudo apt update -y <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> sudo apt upgrade -y
 sudo apt install wget -y</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">2.Download and install Chrome Remote Desktop</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=" sudo wget https://dl.google.com/linux/direct/chrome-remote-desktop_current_amd64.deb
 sudo apt install ./chrome-remote-desktop_current_amd64.deb -y "><pre> sudo wget https://dl.google.com/linux/direct/chrome-remote-desktop_current_amd64.deb
 sudo apt install ./chrome-remote-desktop_current_amd64.deb -y </pre></div>
<ol start="3" dir="auto">
<li>installing XFCE Desktop Environment
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sudo DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
 apt install --assume-yes xfce4 desktop-base dbus-x11 xscreensaver"><pre>sudo DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive \
 apt install --assume-yes xfce4 desktop-base dbus-x11 xscreensaver</pre></div>
</li>
<li>Activating Chrome Remote Desktop
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=" sudo bash -c 'echo &quot;exec /etc/X11/Xsession /usr/bin/xfce4-session&quot; &gt; /etc/chrome-remote-desktop-session'"><pre> sudo bash -c <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>echo "exec /etc/X11/Xsession /usr/bin/xfce4-session" &gt; /etc/chrome-remote-desktop-session<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>Disabling lightdm.service</li>
</ol>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=" sudo systemctl disable lightdm.service"><pre> sudo systemctl disable lightdm.service</pre></div>
<h1 tabindex="-1" id="user-content-step-four" dir="auto"><a class="heading-link" href="#step-four">Step Four<svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></h1> 
   - Download Chrome Remote Desktop app/Extensions or Go to <a href="https://remotedesktop.google.com" rel="nofollow">Chrome Remote Desktop</a>
